		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Brazilian footballer</div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">For other people named Marquinhos, see <a href="/wiki/Marquinhos_(disambiguation)" class="mw-disambig" title="Marquinhos (disambiguation)">Marquinhos (disambiguation)</a>.</div>
<p class="mw-empty-elt">

</p>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">This name uses <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_name" title="Portuguese name">Portuguese naming customs</a>: the first or maternal <a href="/wiki/Surname" title="Surname">family name</a> is <i>Aoás</i>&#32;and the second or paternal family name is <i>Corrêa</i>.</div>

<p><b>Marcos Aoás Corrêa</b> (born 14 May 1994), commonly known as <b>Marquinhos</b> (<span style="font-size:85%;">Brazilian Portuguese:&#160;</span><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Portuguese" title="Help:IPA/Portuguese">[makjus]</a></span>), is a Brazilian professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Centre-back" title="Defender (association football)">defender</a> for <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> club <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a>, whom he captains, and the <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil national team</a>. Mainly a <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Centre-back" title="Defender (association football)">central defender</a>, he can also play as a <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Full-back" title="Defender (association football)">right-back</a> or a <a href="/wiki/Defensive_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Defensive midfielder">defensive midfielder</a>.
</p><p>He began his career at <a href="/wiki/Sport_Club_Corinthians_Paulista" title="Sport Club Corinthians Paulista">Corinthians</a>, and after winning the <a href="/wiki/2012_Copa_Libertadores" title="2012 Copa Libertadores">2012 Copa Libertadores</a> he moved to <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">Roma</a> for an eventual fee of 3&#160;million. Marquinhos was a regular in his only season as Roma reached the <a href="/wiki/2013_Coppa_Italia_Final" title="2013 Coppa Italia Final">Coppa Italia Final</a>. In July 2013, he moved to Paris Saint-Germain for 31.4&#160;million on a five-year contract, one of the highest fees for a player under the age of 20.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcfee_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcfee-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-skyfee_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-skyfee-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-tenfee_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-tenfee-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> He has won 23 trophies at the club, including six <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> titles. Marquinhos played less frequently after the acquisition of compatriot <a href="/wiki/David_Luiz" title="David Luiz">David Luiz</a> in 2014,<sup id="cite_ref-alex_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-alex-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-silva_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-silva-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> returning to an integral role after the latter was sold in 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-johnson_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-johnson-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Marquinhos made his full international debut for Brazil in 2013, and was part of their <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_under-20_football_team" title="Brazil national under-20 football team">Under-21 side</a> which won the <a href="/wiki/2014_Toulon_Tournament" title="2014 Toulon Tournament">2014 Toulon Tournament</a>. He also represented the nation at the <a href="/wiki/2015_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2015 Copa América">2015 Copa América</a> and the following year's <a href="/wiki/Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_Centenario" title="Copa América Centenario">Copa América Centenario</a>, and won a gold medal at the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2016_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Football at the 2016 Summer Olympics  Men&#39;s tournament">2016 Olympics</a>, and took part at the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> and subsequently the <a href="/wiki/2019_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2019 Copa América">2019 Copa América</a>, winning the latter title.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Corinthians">Corinthians</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Corinthians">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Marquinhos joined Corinthians at the age of eight in 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> After winning the state junior cup, he was first included in a senior matchday squad on 29 January 2012,<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> remaining an unused substitute in their 10 home win over <a href="/wiki/Clube_Atl%C3%A9tico_Linense" title="Clube Atlético Linense">Linense</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Campeonato_Paulista" title="Campeonato Paulista">Campeonato Paulista</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> He made his professional debut in the competition on 18 February, playing the full 90 minutes of a victory by the same score at <a href="/wiki/Associa%C3%A7%C3%A3o_Desportiva_S%C3%A3o_Caetano" title="Associação Desportiva São Caetano">São Caetano</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He made eight appearances across <a href="/wiki/2012_Campeonato_Paulista" title="2012 Campeonato Paulista">the season</a>, as the <i>Timão</i> topped the table in the regular season but were defeated by <a href="/wiki/Associa%C3%A7%C3%A3o_Atl%C3%A9tica_Ponte_Preta" title="Associação Atlética Ponte Preta">Ponte Preta</a> in the play-offs quarter-finals.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the conclusion of the state championship, Marquinhos made his <a href="/wiki/Campeonato_Brasileiro_S%C3%A9rie_A" title="Campeonato Brasileiro Série A">Campeonato Brasileiro Série A</a> debut on 20 May 2012, playing the full 90 minutes in a 01 loss to <a href="/wiki/Fluminense_FC" title="Fluminense FC">Fluminense</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Paulo_Machado_de_Carvalho_Stadium" class="mw-redirect" title="Paulo Machado de Carvalho Stadium">Paulo Machado de Carvalho Stadium</a>; both teams were resting players in the first game of <a href="/wiki/2012_Campeonato_Brasileiro_S%C3%A9rie_A" title="2012 Campeonato Brasileiro Série A">the season</a> due to concentration on the <a href="/wiki/Copa_Libertadores" title="Copa Libertadores">Copa Libertadores</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> He played six games in the national championship,<sup id="cite_ref-Marquinhos_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Marquinhos-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> and was an unused substitute as the club won the <a href="/wiki/2012_Copa_Libertadores_Finals" title="2012 Copa Libertadores Finals">2012 Copa Libertadores Finals</a> against <a href="/wiki/Boca_Juniors" title="Boca Juniors">Boca Juniors</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Roma">Roma</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Roma">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In July 2012, Marquinhos was signed by Italian club <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">Roma</a> from Corinthians. The transfer was initially a one-year loan for a fee of 1.5&#160;million, rising to 3&#160;million after he made eight first-team appearances of at least 45 minutes each.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> At Roma, he played under the name "Marcos" printed on his jersey to avoid confusion with teammate <a href="/wiki/Marquinho_(footballer,_born_1986)" class="mw-redirect" title="Marquinho (footballer, born 1986)">Marquinho</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-voce_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-voce-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Marquinhos made his debut on 16 September in a 23 loss against <a href="/wiki/Bologna_F.C._1909" title="Bologna F.C. 1909">Bologna</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Stadio_Olimpico" title="Stadio Olimpico">Stadio Olimpico</a>, sent on by manager <a href="/wiki/Zden%C4%9Bk_Zeman" title="Zdenk Zeman">Zdenk Zeman</a> to replace <a href="/wiki/Iv%C3%A1n_Piris" title="Iván Piris">Iván Piris</a> for the match's final 15 minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> By October, Zeman decided to partner Marquinhos for his speed alongside former Corinthians teammate and fellow Brazilian <a href="/wiki/Leandro_Cast%C3%A1n" title="Leandro Castán">Leandro Castán</a> in central defence, demoting former starter <a href="/wiki/Nicol%C3%A1s_Burdisso" title="Nicolás Burdisso">Nicolás Burdisso</a> to the substitutes' bench.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> He given a straight red card in a 42 victory over <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a> on 22 December when he was judged to have denied <a href="/wiki/Stephan_El_Shaarawy" title="Stephan El Shaarawy">Stephan El Shaarawy</a> a clear goalscoring opportunity.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Marquinhos played 26 <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> games in his only season, and four in the <a href="/wiki/Coppa_Italia" title="Coppa Italia">Coppa Italia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Marquinhos_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Marquinhos-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> This included the full 90 minutes of the <a href="/wiki/2013_Coppa_Italia_Final" title="2013 Coppa Italia Final">final</a> on 26 May, playing at right back as Roma lost 01 to <a href="/wiki/Derby_della_Capitale" title="Derby della Capitale">Rome rivals</a> <a href="/wiki/S.S._Lazio" title="S.S. Lazio">Lazio</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Paris_Saint-Germain">Paris Saint-Germain</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Paris Saint-Germain">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatleft" style="width:25%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:"  ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:"  ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">I am delighted to be joining Paris Saint-Germain, a club where so many Brazilians have played and helped write the club's history. I'm going to do all I can to continue that tradition, and take my turn to write some great pages of the club's history. Paris Saint-Germain is going to allow me to improve alongside some exceptional players with the hope of winning trophies and the hearts of the supporters.</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style=""> Marquinhos speaking of his transfer.<sup id="cite_ref-espn_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-espn-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<h4><span id="2013.E2.80.9314:_Transfer_and_debut_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201314:_Transfer_and_debut_season">201314: Transfer and debut season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 201314: Transfer and debut season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 19 July 2013, Marquinhos signed a five-year deal with French side <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> for a fee of 31.4&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-espn_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-espn-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>  According to <a href="/wiki/BBC_Sport" title="BBC Sport">BBC Sport</a>, this was then the highest transfer fee for a teenager,<sup id="cite_ref-bbcfee_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcfee-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> although <a href="/wiki/Sky_Sports" title="Sky Sports">Sky Sports</a> report it as then the fifth-highest such transfer,<sup id="cite_ref-skyfee_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-skyfee-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> and France's Le 10 Sport record it as the third-highest.<sup id="cite_ref-tenfee_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-tenfee-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> French news channel <a href="/wiki/BFM_TV" title="BFM TV">BFM TV</a> described the transfer as the fifth most expensive of all time for a defender, after those of <a href="/wiki/Rio_Ferdinand" title="Rio Ferdinand">Rio Ferdinand</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thiago_Silva" title="Thiago Silva">Thiago Silva</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lilian_Thuram" title="Lilian Thuram">Lilian Thuram</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dani_Alves" title="Dani Alves">Dani Alves</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Marquinhos' transfer was threatened by anomalies in his medical exam,<sup id="cite_ref-espn_22-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-espn-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> and he missed the team's pre-season visit to Sweden. His mother said that he had caught a virus,<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> with PSG denying claims circulated by <i><a href="/wiki/Le_Parisien" title="Le Parisien">Le Parisien</a></i> that he had <a href="/wiki/Hepatitis" title="Hepatitis">hepatitis</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
On his official debut for the club on 17 September, Marquinhos scored his first professional goal to confirm a 41 win against <a href="/wiki/Olympiacos_F.C." title="Olympiacos F.C.">Olympiacos</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Karaiskakis_Stadium" title="Karaiskakis Stadium">Karaiskakis Stadium</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="201314 UEFA Champions League group stage">group stage</a> of the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201314 UEFA Champions League">201314 UEFA Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Five days later, Marquinhos made his <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> debut as a starter in a 11 draw against <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco_FC" title="AS Monaco FC">Monaco</a>. His first league goal for the club came on 28 September, the first in a 20 win over <a href="/wiki/Toulouse_FC" title="Toulouse FC">Toulouse</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> On 2 October, he scored the second goal in a 30 Champions League group victory against <a href="/wiki/S.L._Benfica" title="S.L. Benfica">Benfica</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> Marquinhos, who was playing due to injury to Thiago Silva, expressed surprise at his goalscoring form at the start of his PSG career.<sup id="cite_ref-blanc_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-blanc-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> Marquinhos scored the last goal of PSG's 61 aggregate win over <a href="/wiki/Bayer_04_Leverkusen" title="Bayer 04 Leverkusen">Bayer Leverkusen</a> in the last 16 of the Champions League on 12 March 2014,<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> and was an unused substitute as they won the <a href="/wiki/2014_Coupe_de_la_Ligue_Final" title="2014 Coupe de la Ligue Final">Coupe de la Ligue final</a> against <a href="/wiki/Olympique_Lyonnais" title="Olympique Lyonnais">Lyon</a> on 19 April.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> On 10 May, he scored the opening goal of a 31 win over <a href="/wiki/Lille_OSC" title="Lille OSC">Lille</a>, which put by-then league champions PSG to a record league points tally of 86 with a game left to play.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2014.E2.80.9315:_First_domestic_treble"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201415:_First_domestic_treble">201415: First domestic treble</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 201415: First domestic treble">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Marquinhos began the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C._season" title="201415 Paris Saint-Germain F.C. season">201415 season</a> on 2 August in the <a href="/wiki/2014_Troph%C3%A9e_des_Champions" title="2014 Trophée des Champions">Trophée des Champions</a>, playing the whole 90 minutes as PSG won 20 against <a href="/wiki/En_Avant_de_Guingamp" class="mw-redirect" title="En Avant de Guingamp">Guingamp</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Workers_Stadium" class="mw-redirect" title="Workers Stadium">Workers Stadium</a> in <a href="/wiki/Beijing" title="Beijing">Beijing</a>. In the 32nd minute, he gave away a <a href="/wiki/Penalty_kick_(association_football)" title="Penalty kick (association football)">penalty kick</a> by fouling <a href="/wiki/Claudio_Beauvue" title="Claudio Beauvue">Claudio Beauvue</a>, but <a href="/wiki/Salvatore_Sirigu" title="Salvatore Sirigu">Salvatore Sirigu</a> saved the penalty shot from <a href="/wiki/Mustapha_Yatabar%C3%A9" title="Mustapha Yatabaré">Mustapha Yatabaré</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> His first goal of the season came in a 20 win at <a href="/wiki/Stade_Malherbe_Caen" title="Stade Malherbe Caen">Caen</a> on 24 September, heading in <a href="/wiki/Javier_Pastore" title="Javier Pastore">Javier Pastore</a>'s corner.<sup id="cite_ref-Marquinhos_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Marquinhos-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> On 26 March 2015, Marquinhos signed a one-year contract extension to keep him at the team until 2019. Club president <a href="/wiki/Nasser_Al-Khelaifi" title="Nasser Al-Khelaifi">Nasser Al-Khelaifi</a> said that, "The biggest European clubs were interested in signing Marquinhos, so this contract extension further reinforces Paris Saint-Germains ambitious long-term project."<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> As the right-back in an all-Brazilian defence (alongside <a href="/wiki/Maxwell_(footballer,_born_1981)" title="Maxwell (footballer, born 1981)">Maxwell</a>, Thiago Silva and <a href="/wiki/David_Luiz" title="David Luiz">David Luiz</a>), Marquinhos featured in PSG's 32 win at <a href="/wiki/Olympique_de_Marseille" title="Olympique de Marseille">Marseille</a> in <i><a href="/wiki/Le_Classique" title="Le Classique">Le Classique</a></i>, scoring the equaliser.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> Six days later, he started in the 40 victory over <a href="/wiki/SC_Bastia" title="SC Bastia">Bastia</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2015_Coupe_de_la_Ligue_Final" title="2015 Coupe de la Ligue Final">2015 Coupe de la Ligue</a>, his 34th consecutive game without a defeat for the club, surpassing a record set by <a href="/wiki/George_Weah" title="George Weah">George Weah</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> On 16 May, PSG won their third consecutive league title with a 21 victory at <a href="/wiki/Montpellier_HSC" title="Montpellier HSC">Montpellier</a>, with Marquinhos playing the final 12 minutes in place of <a href="/wiki/Yohan_Cabaye" title="Yohan Cabaye">Yohan Cabaye</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Two weeks later, he was an unused substitute as the team finished a perfect domestic season with victory in the <a href="/wiki/2015_Coupe_de_France_Final" title="2015 Coupe de France Final">Coupe de France final</a> against <a href="/wiki/AJ_Auxerre" title="AJ Auxerre">Auxerre</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9316:_Transfer_drama_and_cup_finals"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201516:_Transfer_drama_and_cup_finals">201516: Transfer drama and cup finals</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 201516: Transfer drama and cup finals">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Chelsea_1_PSG_2_(25672641705).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Chelsea_1_PSG_2_%2825672641705%29.jpg/220px-Chelsea_1_PSG_2_%2825672641705%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="220" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Chelsea_1_PSG_2_%2825672641705%29.jpg/330px-Chelsea_1_PSG_2_%2825672641705%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Chelsea_1_PSG_2_%2825672641705%29.jpg/440px-Chelsea_1_PSG_2_%2825672641705%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3064" data-file-height="3064" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Chelsea_1_PSG_2_(25672641705).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Marquinhos (in white, number 5) in a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> in March 2016</div></div></div>
<p>PSG began the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C._season" title="201516 Paris Saint-Germain F.C. season">201516 season</a> with a 20 victory over Lyon in the <a href="/wiki/2015_Troph%C3%A9e_des_Champions" title="2015 Trophée des Champions">2015 Trophée des Champions</a>, with Marquinhos an unused substitute as <a href="/wiki/Serge_Aurier" title="Serge Aurier">Serge Aurier</a> played at right back.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the summer transfer window, <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> had two bids rejected for his signature, of amounts between £25.7£40.4&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Marquinhos rarely started during the season, due to the partnership of his compatriots Silva and David Luiz in the centre of the PSG defence. One of the team's former defenders, <a href="/wiki/Alex_(footballer,_born_1982)" title="Alex (footballer, born 1982)">Alex</a>, recommended that Marquinhos leave the team, as he was in demand from big teams in which he would have an opportunity to play.<sup id="cite_ref-alex_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-alex-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> In February 2016, Silva criticised the agency representing Marquinhos and David Luiz for having led two players of the same position to the same club, thus limiting Marquinhos' opportunities; Silva mentioned <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a>'s interest in the player.<sup id="cite_ref-silva_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-silva-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>  PSG manager <a href="/wiki/Laurent_Blanc" title="Laurent Blanc">Laurent Blanc</a> stated that he would be open for Marquinhos to leave at the end of the season, while agent Giuliano Bertolucci confirmed that Marquinhos would be leaving.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 2 March, Marquinhos scored his first goal of the season as PSG won 31 at <a href="/wiki/A.S._Saint-%C3%89tienne" class="mw-redirect" title="A.S. Saint-Étienne">Saint-Étienne</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Coupe_de_France" title="201516 Coupe de France">cup quarter-finals</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Marquinhos_14-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Marquinhos-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> On 23 April, he played the entirety of a 21 win over Lille in the <a href="/wiki/2016_Coupe_de_la_Ligue_Final" title="2016 Coupe de la Ligue Final">2016 Coupe de la Ligue Final</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-cdll_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cdll-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> and he did so again on 21 May in the <a href="/wiki/2016_Coupe_de_France_Final" title="2016 Coupe de France Final">Coupe de France final</a>, a 42 win over Marseille, as PSG won all four domestic trophies for the second consecutive season.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9317:_Le_Classique_goal_and_contract_negotiations"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201617:_Le_Classique_goal_and_contract_negotiations">201617: <i>Le Classique</i> goal and contract negotiations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 201617: Le Classique goal and contract negotiations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Marquinhos missed PSG's victory in the <a href="/wiki/2016_Troph%C3%A9e_des_Champions" title="2016 Trophée des Champions">2016 Trophée des Champions</a> in August due to his selection in the Brazil team at the Olympics.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> He was tipped by <a href="/wiki/ESPN" title="ESPN">ESPN</a> journalist Jonathan Johnson to play more frequently over the season, as new manager <a href="/wiki/Unai_Emery" title="Unai Emery">Unai Emery</a> sold David Luiz back to Chelsea.<sup id="cite_ref-johnson_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-johnson-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first goal of the season on 26 February 2017, opening a 51 win at rivals Marseille;<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> prior to the game he confirmed that he was in talks for a new contract at the club.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> On 26 April, he scored the last goal of a 50 home win over title rivals <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco_FC" title="AS Monaco FC">Monaco</a> in the Coupe de France semi-finals,<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> and he started beside Silva in a 10 win over <a href="/wiki/Angers_SCO" title="Angers SCO">Angers</a> a month later in <a href="/wiki/2017_Coupe_de_France_Final" title="2017 Coupe de France Final">the final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Marquinhos said on 14 May that there was a "100 percent" chance he would remain at the club the following season.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318.2C_2018.E2.80.9319:_Domestic_success"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201718,_201819:_Domestic_success">201718, 201819: Domestic success</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 201718, 201819: Domestic success">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Marquinhos began the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C._season" title="201718 Paris Saint-Germain F.C. season">201718 season</a> on 29 July, starting as PSG won 21 in the <a href="/wiki/2017_Troph%C3%A9e_des_Champions" title="2017 Trophée des Champions">2017 Trophée des Champions</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Stade_de_Tanger" class="mw-redirect" title="Grand Stade de Tanger">Grand Stade de Tanger</a> in Morocco.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> In the team's victorious run in the Coupe de la Ligue, he scored in the 32 semi-final win at <a href="/wiki/Stade_Rennais_F.C." title="Stade Rennais F.C.">Rennes</a> on 30 January 2018,<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> but was unused in the <a href="/wiki/2018_Coupe_de_la_Ligue_Final" title="2018 Coupe de la Ligue Final">30 final win</a> over Monaco as young local <a href="/wiki/Presnel_Kimpembe" title="Presnel Kimpembe">Presnel Kimpembe</a> took his place.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> PSG won all four domestic competitions over the season, and Marquinhos told <i><a href="/wiki/Le_Figaro" title="Le Figaro">Le Figaro</a></i> at the end of the campaign that he would remain at the club.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320:_European_final"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201920:_European_final">201920: European final</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 201920: European final">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 12 August 2020, Marquinhos scored a late equalizer against <a href="/wiki/Atalanta_B.C." title="Atalanta B.C.">Atalanta</a> in the Champions League quarter-finals, sparking a late comeback for PSG to win 21.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> On 18 August, Marquinhos scored in a 30 win over <a href="/wiki/RB_Leipzig" title="RB Leipzig">RB Leipzig</a> in the semi-finals of the competition, which saw PSG reach the <a href="/wiki/2020_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2020 UEFA Champions League Final">Champions League final</a> for the first time in its history.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> PSG eventually lost out 10 to <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> on 23 August.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321:_Club_captaincy"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="202021:_Club_captaincy">202021: Club captaincy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 202021: Club captaincy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Marquinhos was appointed as PSG's <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">club captain</a> on 15 September 2020, succeeding Thiago Silva in the role.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first goal of the season in a match against <a href="/wiki/OGC_Nice" title="OGC Nice">Nice</a> five days later.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> On 2 December, Marquinhos scored the second goal for PSG in a 31 win against <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Champions_League" title="202021 UEFA Champions League">group stage</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In January 2021, Marquinhos played his 300th PSG game against Marseille, also entering the club's top 10 appearance makers of all time.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Youth_and_first_caps">Youth and first caps</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Youth and first caps">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Marquinhos played every minute of Brazil's campaign at the <a href="/wiki/2011_South_American_Under-17_Football_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="2011 South American Under-17 Football Championship">2011 South American Under-17 Football Championship</a>, as they won and qualified for <a href="/wiki/2011_FIFA_U-17_World_Cup" title="2011 FIFA U-17 World Cup">that year's World Cup in that category</a>. He was again an undisputed starter except for one match at that tournament, as the team took fourth place in Mexico.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In October 2013, Marquinhos, who is <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_Brazilian" class="mw-redirect" title="Portuguese Brazilian">of dual Portuguese and Brazilian nationality</a>, stated that he would be open to representing the <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_football_team" title="Portugal national football team">Portugal national team</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> However, later that month, he received his first call-up for <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a> when <a href="/wiki/Luiz_Felipe_Scolari" title="Luiz Felipe Scolari">Luiz Felipe Scolari</a> named his squad for friendly matches against <a href="/wiki/Honduras_national_football_team" title="Honduras national football team">Honduras</a> and <a href="/wiki/Chile_national_football_team" title="Chile national football team">Chile</a> to be played that November.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> He made his debut against Honduras in <a href="/wiki/Miami" title="Miami">Miami</a> on 17 November, replacing David Luiz for the last 20 minutes of a 50 win.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Marquinhos played for <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_under-20_football_team" title="Brazil national under-20 football team">Brazil Under-21</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2014_Toulon_Tournament" title="2014 Toulon Tournament">2014 Toulon Tournament</a>, featuring in all five of their matches as the country won the tournament. He scored to put Brazil 32 up in their eventual 52 win in the final over <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-20_football_team" title="France national under-20 football team">France</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2016:_Olympic_gold_and_Copa_Am.C3.A9rica_Centenario"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016:_Olympic_gold_and_Copa_América_Centenario">2016: Olympic gold and Copa América Centenario</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: 2016: Olympic gold and Copa América Centenario">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Brasil_conquista_primeiro_ouro_ol%C3%ADmpico_nos_penaltis_1039261-20082016-_mg_4249.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Brasil_conquista_primeiro_ouro_ol%C3%ADmpico_nos_penaltis_1039261-20082016-_mg_4249.jpg/220px-Brasil_conquista_primeiro_ouro_ol%C3%ADmpico_nos_penaltis_1039261-20082016-_mg_4249.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Brasil_conquista_primeiro_ouro_ol%C3%ADmpico_nos_penaltis_1039261-20082016-_mg_4249.jpg/330px-Brasil_conquista_primeiro_ouro_ol%C3%ADmpico_nos_penaltis_1039261-20082016-_mg_4249.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Brasil_conquista_primeiro_ouro_ol%C3%ADmpico_nos_penaltis_1039261-20082016-_mg_4249.jpg/440px-Brasil_conquista_primeiro_ouro_ol%C3%ADmpico_nos_penaltis_1039261-20082016-_mg_4249.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3800" data-file-height="2533" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Brasil_conquista_primeiro_ouro_ol%C3%ADmpico_nos_penaltis_1039261-20082016-_mg_4249.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Marquinhos (second from left) celebrating Brazil's gold medal at the 2016 Olympics</div></div></div>
<p>After missing the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a> on home soil, Marquinhos returned to the senior side in September 2014 under new manager <a href="/wiki/Dunga" title="Dunga">Dunga</a>. He featured in friendly wins over <a href="/wiki/Colombia_national_football_team" title="Colombia national football team">Colombia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ecuador_national_football_team" title="Ecuador national football team">Ecuador</a> in <a href="/wiki/Miami" title="Miami">Miami</a>, making his first start against the latter.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-nft_70-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nft-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> Marquinhos was included in the Brazilian squad for the <a href="/wiki/2015_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2015 Copa América">2015 Copa América</a> in Chile, his first major international tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> He made his competitive debut  and only appearance in the tournament  on 21 June in their final <a href="/wiki/2015_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_Group_C" title="2015 Copa América Group C">group match</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Estadio_Monumental_David_Arellano" title="Estadio Monumental David Arellano">Estadio Monumental David Arellano</a>, replacing <a href="/wiki/Robinho" title="Robinho">Robinho</a> for the final 14 minutes of a 21 win over <a href="/wiki/Venezuela_national_football_team" title="Venezuela national football team">Venezuela</a> which sent Brazil into the quarter-finals as group winners.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2016, Marquinhos was named in the Brazilian squad for the <a href="/wiki/Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_Centenario" title="Copa América Centenario">Copa América Centenario</a> in the United States, an "experimental" selection lacking his Paris Saint-Germain defensive partners Thiago Silva and David Luiz.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> He played in the first two games at centre-back alongside <a href="/wiki/Gil_(footballer,_born_1987)" title="Gil (footballer, born 1987)">Gil</a> before being replaced by <a href="/wiki/Miranda_(footballer,_born_1984)" title="Miranda (footballer, born 1984)">Miranda</a> for the last group game, a 10 loss to <a href="/wiki/Peru_national_football_team" title="Peru national football team">Peru</a> at <a href="/wiki/Gillette_Stadium" title="Gillette Stadium">Gillette Stadium</a> that eliminated his team.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> Later that year, he was included in the squad for the team's hosting of the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2016_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Football at the 2016 Summer Olympics  Men&#39;s tournament">Olympic tournament</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> and in the semi-final against <a href="/wiki/Honduras_national_under-23_football_team" title="Honduras national under-23 football team">Honduras</a> in <a href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro" title="Rio de Janeiro">Rio de Janeiro</a>, he scored in an eventual 60 win.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2018_World_Cup_and_2019_Copa_Am.C3.A9rica_victory"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018_World_Cup_and_2019_Copa_América_victory">2018 World Cup and 2019 Copa América victory</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: 2018 World Cup and 2019 Copa América victory">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>With Silva injured, Marquinhos captained Brazil for the first time on 10 October 2017 in a 30 win over <a href="/wiki/Chile_national_football_team" title="Chile national football team">Chile</a> at <a href="/wiki/Allianz_Parque" title="Allianz Parque">Allianz Parque</a> in his hometown. Brazil had already qualified for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> and the result ended the continental champion opponents' hope of qualification.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> In May 2018 he was named in manager <a href="/wiki/Tite_(football_manager)" title="Tite (football manager)">Tite</a>s 23-man squad for the final tournament in Russia, alongside clubmates Silva and <a href="/wiki/Neymar" title="Neymar">Neymar</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first international goal on 11 September, in a 50 friendly win over <a href="/wiki/El_Salvador_national_football_team" title="El Salvador national football team">El Salvador</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In May 2019, Marquinhos was included in Brazil's 23-man squad for the <a href="/wiki/2019_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2019 Copa América">2019 Copa América</a> on home soil.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> In the semi-finals against <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a> on 2 July, Marquinhos was tasked with marking <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a> while suffering from <a href="/wiki/Diarrhea" title="Diarrhea">diarrhea</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> He helped Brazil to a 20 victory over their rivals; he came off in second half for <a href="/wiki/Miranda_(footballer,_born_1984)" title="Miranda (footballer, born 1984)">Miranda</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> On 7 July, Marquinhos started in Brazil's 31 win over Peru in the <a href="/wiki/2019_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_Final" title="2019 Copa América Final">final</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Maracan%C3%A3_Stadium" title="Maracanã Stadium">Maracanã Stadium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 9 October 2020, Marquinhos scored his first competitive goal for Brazil, heading the opener of a 50 win over <a href="/wiki/Bolivia_national_football_team" title="Bolivia national football team">Bolivia</a> at Corinthians' ground, in <a href="/wiki/2022_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification" title="2022 FIFA World Cup qualification">2022 FIFA World Cup qualification</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> The following month, he earned his 50th cap in another qualifier against Venezuela.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Thiago_Silva_%26_Marquinhos.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Thiago_Silva_%26_Marquinhos.jpg/170px-Thiago_Silva_%26_Marquinhos.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="291" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Thiago_Silva_%26_Marquinhos.jpg/255px-Thiago_Silva_%26_Marquinhos.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Thiago_Silva_%26_Marquinhos.jpg/340px-Thiago_Silva_%26_Marquinhos.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1512" data-file-height="2584" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Thiago_Silva_%26_Marquinhos.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Marquinhos (right) has been likened to <a href="/wiki/Thiago_Silva" title="Thiago Silva">Thiago Silva</a> (left), who was his club and international teammate.</div></div></div>
<p>In terms of his playing position, Marquinhos is predominantly deployed as a <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Centre-back" title="Defender (association football)">central defender</a>, but has also been used at <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Full-back" title="Defender (association football)">right-back</a> and in a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Central_midfielder" title="Midfielder">central</a> or <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Defensive_midfielder" title="Midfielder">defensive midfield</a> role.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> He is noted for his anticipation, pace, and intelligence, as well as his technical skills, composure, passing ability, elegance on the ball, and confidence in possession, which enables him to break down attacks and subsequently play the ball out or start offensive plays from the back.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On signing for Roma, Marquinhos described himself as a quick player, with a good positional sense, who wins back a lot of balls, and who knows how to impose himself on a game due to his ability to start attacking plays from the back. He named Thiago Silva as his role model.<sup id="cite_ref-voce_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-voce-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> In March 2015, Marquinhos told <i><a href="/wiki/FourFourTwo" title="FourFourTwo">FourFourTwo</a></i> that he compensated for his average height for a defender by honing his strength and timing, attributes he learnt from PSG assistant manager <a href="/wiki/Claude_Mak%C3%A9l%C3%A9l%C3%A9" title="Claude Makélélé">Claude Makélélé</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> He praised manager Laurent Blanc, a former defender himself, for encouraging the PSG defenders to attack in <a href="/wiki/Set_piece_(football)" title="Set piece (football)">set pieces</a> and teaching them the correct positioning in that situation.<sup id="cite_ref-blanc_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-blanc-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Fellow Roma defender Nicolás Burdisso said in August 2012 that Marquinhos was "a little phenomenon. He has speed, heading ability, he knows what to do, he is humble. He is a little Thiago Silva".<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In January 2014, Marquinhos was named by British newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/The_Observer" title="The Observer">The Observer</a></i> as one of the ten most promising young players in Europe. They wrote, "He has the temperament to remain undaunted, the talent to succeed, and could benefit from playing alongside his club team-mate, Thiago Silva, with whom he enjoys a solid understanding at wealthy Paris Saint-Germain."<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In May 2015, Marquinhos told <i>Le Parisien</i> that he had become engaged to Brazilian singer and reality television contestant Carol Cabrino. He proposed to her underneath the <a href="/wiki/Eiffel_Tower" title="Eiffel Tower">Eiffel Tower</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> They had a civil wedding in June 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> Their daughter was born on 1 November 2017, with Cabrino having gone early into labour while watching Marquinhos playing a Champions League match against <a href="/wiki/R.S.C._Anderlecht" title="R.S.C. Anderlecht">Anderlecht</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Parc_des_Princes" title="Parc des Princes">Parc des Princes</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> Their son was born in December 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In September 2020 he tested positive for <a href="/wiki/Coronavirus_disease_2019" class="mw-redirect" title="Coronavirus disease 2019">COVID-19</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During a match between PSG and <a href="/wiki/FC_Nantes" title="FC Nantes">Nantes</a> on 14 March 2021, Marquinhos' parents were held hostage in a robbery. His teammate <a href="/wiki/%C3%81ngel_Di_Mar%C3%ADa" title="Ángel Di María">Ángel Di María</a> was in a similar situation, with his family being hostage in a robbery as well.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Marquinhos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
